IV is a metric used by traders to predict future fluctuations in the price of an asset. Following the fake news, major expiry option IVs for Bitcoin increased over the three-month period. Short- and medium-term IVs rose 5% overall, while ultra-short-term IVs rose nearly 20%. However, long-term option IVs expiring at year-end and beyond remain largely unchanged.\n\n\ud83d\udca5Generally, an increase in IV indicates that the market expects the price of the asset in question to move significantly.\n\nInterestingly, Ethereum (ETH) seems unaffected by this market turmoil. IVs across all major futures of ETH remained stable, indicating that the market movement was entirely due to Bitcoin ETF fake news.\n\nA closer look at the distribution of options trades shows that all the upside for Bitcoin came from short-term buying in the 28,000 to 30,000 range, according to the analyst.
